    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index + 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
                b = a.next
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #  _____    _____    _____
                # |  A  |  |  C  |->|  B |
                # |_____|  |_____|<-|____|
>               b.prev = c
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'prev'

data = <linkedList1.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7f5f0947a9e0>, index = 2

    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index << 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
>               b = a.next
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'next'

    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index | 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
                b = a.next
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #  _____    _____    _____
                # |  A  |  |  C  |->|  B |
                # |_____|  |_____|<-|____|
>               b.prev = c
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'prev'

self = <linkedList1.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7f3d3a5d7130>, data = None
index = -440

    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index - 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
                b = a.next
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #  _____    _____    _____
                # |  A  |  |  C  |->|  B |
                # |_____|  |_____|<-|____|
>               b.prev = c
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'prev'

WHOLE_SUITE/test_linkedList1_WHOLE_SUITE.py:128:

self = <linkedList1.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7f61ab3e0a60>, data = None
index = -440

    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index - 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
                b = a.next
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #  _____    _____    _____
                # |  A  |  |  C  |->|  B |
                # |_____|  |_____|<-|____|
>               b.prev = c
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'prev'

self = <linkedList1.DoublyLinkedList object at 0x7fd9fb116b60>, data = -440
index = -440

    def insert(self, data, index):
        if index >= self.size:
            raise IndexError()
        if not self.head is None:
            self.head = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
            self.cursor = self.head
        else:
            # If this insertion should be an append
            if index == self.size - 1:
                # We've got a method for that!
                self.append(data)
            # If a new head needs to be added
            elif index == 0:
                #              _____   _____
                # self.head|->|  A  | |  C  |
                #           <-|_____| |_____|
                a = self.head
                c = DoublyLinkedNode(data)
    
                #              _____    ______
                # self.head|->|  C  |->|  A  |
                #           <-|_____|<-|_____|
                self.head = c
                c.next = a
                a.prev = c
                self.cursor = self.head
            # It's between two nodes
            else:
                a = self.head
                for x in range(index - 1):
                    a = a.next
                #  _____    _____
                # |  A  |->|  B  |
                # |_____|<-|_____|
>               b = a.next
E               AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute 'next'
